***gaunt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaunt.html>gaunt</a> (75899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">gawnt</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">gawnte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lean, slender</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, probably from a Scandinavian source, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">gandr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">magic staff, stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gandaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stick, staff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷʰen-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to beat, hit, drive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">gandur</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">magic staff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">gand</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tall pointed stick; tall, thin <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">gand</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:gan.html>gan</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">gana</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cut-off tree limbs</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bavarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bavarian language">Bavarian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="bar">Gunten</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of wedge or peg</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related also to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">gūþ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">battle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dēfendō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ward off, defend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">gank</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a lean, emaciated horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaunt.html>gaunt</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">gaunter</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">gauntest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lean, angular<span class="serial-comma">,</span> and bony
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1866</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herman_Melville" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Herman Melville">Herman Melville</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle-Pieces_and_Aspects_of_the_War" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Battle-Pieces and Aspects of the War">Battle-Pieces and Aspects of the War</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/ebooks/12384">[1]</a></sup>, The Portent:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Hanging from the beam,<br /> Slowly swaying (such the law),<br /><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaunt.html>Gaunt</a></b> the shadow on your green,<br /> Shenandoah!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1894</b>,  Joseph Jacobs,  chapter 1, in  <cite>The Fables of Aesop</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://ebooks.adelaide.edu.au/a/aesop/a3j/chapter1.html">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaunt.html>gaunt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wolf.html>Wolf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> almost dead with hunger when he happened to meet a House-dog who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> passing by.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:haggard.html>haggard</a>, drawn<span class="serial-comma">,</span> and emaciated
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1898</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H.G._Wells" class="extiw" title="w:H.G. Wells">H.G. Wells</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_War_of_the_Worlds" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The War of the Worlds">The War of the Worlds</a></cite>, London |  William Heinemann, page 239:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Far away I saw a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaunt.html>gaunt</a></b> cat <a href = vnd.unilang:slink.html>slink</a> crouchingly along a wall, but traces of <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> there <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> none.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1917</b>,  Arthur Conan Doyle,  chapter 5, in  <cite>His Last Bow</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://ebooks.adelaide.edu.au/d/doyle/arthur_conan/d75la/chapter5.html">[3]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In the dim light of a <a href = vnd.unilang:foggy.html>foggy</a> November day the sick room <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a gloomy spot, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaunt.html>gaunt</a></b>, wasted face staring at <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> from the <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> which sent a chill to my heart.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>bleak, barren<span class="serial-comma">,</span> and desolate
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1896</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Baker <a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>Eddy</a>,  “The Way”, in  <cite>Miscellaneous Writings 1883-1896</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://concordexpress.christianscience.com/?query=Mis.%20355:2-4">[4]</a></sup>, page 355:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The present stage of progress in Christian Science presents two opposite aspects, — a full-orbed promise, and a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaunt.html>gaunt</a></b> want.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1908</b>,  William Hope Hodgson,  chapter 14, in  <cite>The House on the Borderland</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://ebooks.adelaide.edu.au/h/hodgson/william_hope/house/chapter14.html">[5]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Behind <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> up, to an extraordinary height, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaunt.html>gaunt</a></b>, black cliffs.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***gauw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gauw.html>gauw</a> (1165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gouwe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gauwe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick, fast, hasty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gâ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gā</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ganhuz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ganhwaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sudden, quick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of unknown origin. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">gau</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick, fast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">jäh</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sudden, abrupt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">gay</span>.
</p>

</p>

<li>soon</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gauwdief.html>gauwdief</a> (93327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gauw.html>gauw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dief.html>dief</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thief</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gauwdief.html>gauwdief</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gauwdieven.html>gauwdieven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gauwdief.html>gauwdiefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fast-fingered, crafty thief</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A clever crook, <a href = vnd.unilang:hustler.html>hustler</a></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:gauwdief.html>gauwdief</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>  <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gāva</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gēbō</i>, ablaut variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gebō</i>.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:gazon.html>gazon</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:gazon.html>gazon</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">gason</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">wason</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">piece of ground covered with grass, turf</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*waso</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ground, turf</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wasô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">moisture; ground</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***gebaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebaar.html>gebaar</a> (5620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaren.html>gebare</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaren.html>gebare</a></i>. Equivalent to a deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaren.html>gebaren</a></i>. The sense “gesture” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> relatively recent and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> likely influenced by the sense “movement” and the related, now obsolete term <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaarde.html>gebaarde</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaar.html>gebaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaren.html>gebaren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebaar.html>gebaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>gesture <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act of gesticulating</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from early 18th c.]</span></li>
<li>gesture <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act or token of appreciation or lack thereof</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> movement, motion
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beweging.html>beweging</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> appearance
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uiterlijk.html>uiterlijk</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> uproar, <a href = vnd.unilang:tumult.html>tumult</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:misbaar.html>misbaar</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rumoer.html>rumoer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tumult.html>tumult</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***gebeuren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebeuren.html>gebeuren</a> (477)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geburen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">geburien</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to happen, occur</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gaburjaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beuren.html>beuren</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">geböhren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to happen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:barre.html>barre</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to happen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġebyrian</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to happen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:gebieden.html>gebieden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gebiodan</i>. ***geboefte.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geboefte.html>geboefte</a> (43776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ge-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boef.html>boef</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crook</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geboefte.html>geboefte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geboefte.html>geboeftes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">geboeften</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> criminals, delinquents, crooks</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scum, rabble</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>boevenvolk, <a href = vnd.unilang:gespuis.html>gespuis</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:geboortedag.html>geboortedag</a> (29954)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geboorte.html>geboorte</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geboortedag.html>geboortedag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geboortedag.html>geboortedagen</a></b>)
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The Dutch language <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> a distinction between the day of one's birth (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geboortedag.html>geboortedag</a></i>) and the annual birth celebration day (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verjaardag.html>verjaardag</a></i>).
